[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Frame offset: [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m40[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Shadow byte representation shows: `f1 f1 f1 f1 [0m[1;36m00[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mf3[0m[1;39m][0m[39mf3 f3`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - f1: Stack left redzone[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - [0m[1;36m00[0m[39m: Addressable memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - f3: Stack right redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbeing overwritten[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The buffer [0m[32m'buf'[0m[39m is declared at line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m of packet-openvpn.c in the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_openvpn_msg_common` function[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m in the same function during a tvb_memcpy call[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The attempted write is [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m bytes, exceeding the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer capacity by [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The fuzzer input that triggers this issue is [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m bytes long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mshown in hex dump at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of the output[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo fully understand and address this vulnerability, the following areas should be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexamined:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **epan/dissectors/packet-openvpn.c**:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m: Declaration and initialization of the [0m[32m'buf'[0m[39m variable[0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The entire `dissect_openvpn_msg_common` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstarting at line [0m[1;36m174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand the buffer usage context[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any size calculations or length validations performed before the memcpy [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **OpenVPN Protocol Handling**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCONVERSATION_OPENVPN, msg_sessionid[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m346[0m[39m:  streaming_reassembly_info = [0m[1;35mconversation_get_proto_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconv, proto_openvpn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m347[0m[39m:  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!streaming_reassembly_info[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m348[0m[39m:    streaming_reassembly_info = [0m[1;35mstreaming_reassembly_info_new[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m349[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mconversation_add_proto_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconv, proto_openvpn, [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstreaming_reassembly_info[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m350[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m351[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m352[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mreassemble_streaming_data_and_call_subdissector[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, pinfo, offset,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m353[0m[39m:    msg_length_remaining, openvpn_tree, parent_tree, msg_reassembly_table,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m354[0m[39m:    streaming_reassembly_info, [0m[1;35mget_virtual_frame_num64[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, pinfo, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m355[0m[39m:    tls_handle, parent_tree, NULL [0m[35m/[0m[39m* should it be tcpinfo if we have it? *[0m[35m/[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"OpenVPN Message"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m356[0m[39m:    &openvpn_frag_items, hf_openvpn_fragment_bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m357[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m358[0m[39m:  return [0m[1;35mtvb_captured_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m359[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code analysis, I've identified a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability** in the OpenVPN dissector at [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-openvpn.[0m[1;92mc:312[0m[39m`. The issue occurs when the code attempts to copy data into [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte stack buffer without proper bounds checking.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests in the following code sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m310[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m314[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwkc_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_ntohs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata_len = msg_length_remaining - wkc_len;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, buf, offset, data_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m LINE [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m: OVERFLOW HERE[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m&buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Multiple critical issues:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Issue**: Line [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m copies `data_len` bytes into the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte `buf` array [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout any validation that `data_len <= [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Integer Underflow**: If `wkc_len > msg_length_remaining`, `data_len` becomes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegative, which when cast to `size_t` for `tvb_memcpy` wraps to a huge positive [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Unnecessary Buffer Copy**: The code unnecessarily copies data to check if it [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarts with [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, when Wireshark provides safe APIs for direct [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomparison[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerable Buffer[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAt line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m: `uint8_t buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only used in the vulnerable code section [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m313[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Not used anywhere else in the function[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Can be safely removed[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Impact on Packet Processing[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe check at lines [0m[1;36m313[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m314[0m[39m attempts to reject packets where the data section starts[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m string. This appears to be a heuristic to filter malformed or test [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpackets in P_CONTROL_HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V3 and P_CONTROL_WKC_V1 opcodes.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the Vulnerable Buffer[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-openvpn.[0m[1;92mc:185[0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the line:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muint8_t buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis buffer is only used in the vulnerable code and is no longer needed after [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplying the safe comparison method.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Replace Unsafe Copy-and-Compare with Safe Direct Comparison[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-openvpn.[0m[1;92mc:312[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m314[0m[39m`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the vulnerable code:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, buf, offset, data_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m&buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith the safe version:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len >= [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m && [0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m7[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification for This Approach[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Uses Wireshark's Safe API**: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is the standard Wireshark API for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe string comparison in packet buffers [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee examples in `packet-beep.[0m[1;92mc:454[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m465[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Eliminates Buffer Overflow**: No fixed-size buffer means no overflow possible[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Handles Integer Underflow**: The `data_len >= [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m` check prevents the comparison[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `data_len` is negative [0m[1;39m([0m[39minteger underflow from line [0m[1;36m311[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `data_len` is too small to contain [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Provides Defense in Depth**: `[0m[1;35mtvb_strneql[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` internally:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Uses `[0m[1;35mensure_contiguous_no_exception[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for safe memory access[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m if insufficient bytes are available[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Never throws exceptions or crashes[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves Original Logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still checks if data starts with [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m to reject such packets[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All subsequent code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m359[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continues to work correctly[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Only [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m lines modified, reducing risk of introducing new bugs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Matches Wireshark Coding Patterns**: Similar safe comparison patterns are used[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `packet-beep.c`, `packet-usbms-bot.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why No Additional Validation is Needed[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**For data_len edge cases:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `data_len < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`: Check is skipped, safe[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If `data_len < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39minteger underflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Check is skipped due to signed comparison,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Later uses of `data_len` in `[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m323[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are safe [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecause Wireshark's proto_tree functions handle invalid lengths gracefully[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**For wkc_len validation:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No separate validation needed for `wkc_len` itself[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Invalid `wkc_len` values will only result in incorrect dissection display, not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The Wireshark proto_tree APIs at lines [0m[1;36m334[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m335[0m[39m handle out-of-range lengths safely[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserved Functionality[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Packet Rejection Logic**: Packets with data starting with [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m are still [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrejected [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **WKC Display**: Lines [0m[1;36m325[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m336[0m[39m continue to display wrapped client key data [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Data Display**: Lines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m323[0m[39m continue to display data section correctly[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **All Opcodes**: No changes to handling of other OpenVPN opcodes[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Existing Tests**: No existing test cases are affected since we're only fixing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma buffer overflow bug[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected** because:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only changes the implementation of the [0m[32m"OpenVPN"[0m[39m string check[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The logical behavior remains identical[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to any API signatures or data structures[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to protocol parsing logic[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `buf` variable was only used in this one location[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
